abandon

[ə'bændən], [ə'bændən]


Image Search
v. 放弃；抛弃；放纵
n. 放纵

give up completely (a course of action, a practice, or a way of thinking).
discontinue (a scheduled event) before completion.
allow oneself to indulge in (a desire or impulse).
complete lack of inhibition or restraint.
"her natural mother had abandoned her at an early age"
"derelict houses were abandoned"
"it was an attempt to persuade businesses not to abandon the area to inner-city deprivation"
"he had clearly abandoned all pretense of trying to succeed"
"against the background of perceived threats, the tour was abandoned"
"abandoning herself to moony fantasies"
"she sings and sways with total abandon"
Those who abandon themselves to despair can not succeed.那些自暴自弃的人无法成功。
Despite some difficulties, they're not going to abandon the plan.尽管他们遇到了一些困难,但并不打算放弃这个计划。
The cruel man abandoned his wife and child.那个狠心的男人抛弃了他的妻儿。
They abandon themselves to drinking.他们沉湎于饮酒。
He signed cheques with careless abandon.他无所顾忌地乱开支票。
The cheerleader waved his arms with wild abandon.拉拉队队长疯狂地挥舞双臂。

"the butterflies aggregate in dense groups"

equity

['ekwəti], ['ekwəti]


Image Search
n. 公平；公正
n. 衡平法；权益；产权；(无固定利息的)股票
the quality of being fair and impartial.
a branch of law that developed alongside common law in order to remedy some of its defects in fairness and justice, formerly administered in special courts.
(in the US, UK, and several other countries) a trade union to which most professional actors belong.
the value of the shares issued by a company.
stocks and shares that carry no fixed interest.
the value of a mortgaged property after deduction of charges against it.
"equity of treatment"
"he owns 62% of the group's equity"
The equity of the referee's decision was accepted by everyone.大家都同意裁判员的公正裁判.
They shared the work of the house with perfect equity.他们很公平地分担屋内的工作。
He seeks after equity all life long.他一生都在追求公正。
The judge has become a model of justice and equity.这位法官已经成了公正正义的楷模。
This became the characteristic idea of classical equity.这成了典型的衡平法所具备的特殊观念。
When the existing laws fail to render a satisfactory judgment, equity applies.当现存的法律不能作出令人满意的判决时衡平法就生效。
The equity of the house needed to be re-valued.这所房子的权益需要进行重新评估。
Thus, owners' equity is equal to the total assets minus the liabilities.因此，所有者权益就等于资产总值减去负债的数额。
Equity theory has a relatively strong following in many countries.产权理论有一相对地强跟随在许多国家。

Deep inside the Earth are very hot molten rocks called lava.地球内部深处是十分炽热的岩浆的岩石熔化物。
As the plates separate, hot molten mantle material flows up to fill the void.随着板块的分开，炽热的熔融地幔物质向上流动，以填充空隙。
Finns have been known to do the same with molten tin and buckets.据说芬兰人也一样，只不过是用铸造的锡块和水桶来玩。
